bod skad du/ gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid nges pa/ bcom ldan 'das dpal kun du bzang po la phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bshad pa'i dus gcig na/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das longs spyod chen po phyogs bcu dus bzhi'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku gsung thugs rdo rje'i bdag nyid ma lus mi lus lus pa med pa thams cad dang so so ma yin tha mi dad dbyer med pa'i rang bzhin te// 'og min gyi gnas mtha' dang dbus med pa na gzhi tshad med pa'i ye shes kyi 'khor lo khyab par gsal ba la ye shes rin po che sna tshogs 'bar ba'i gzhal yas khang // rgya phyogs bcur yongs su ma chad pa/ yon tan dpag tu med par rgyas pa'i phyir gru bzhir gyur pa/ lhag pa'i ye shes rin po che'i glo 'bur gyis mdzes pa/ rtse mo phyogs bcu dus bzhi'i sangs rgyas kyi dkyil 'khor ma lus pa thams cad so so ma yin ngo bo nyid gcig pa'i ye shes kun du 'khyil pa/ ye shes bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i rin po che dbyibs dang kha dog la sogs te// rnam pa tha dad pa'i bye brag dang khyad par du gyur pa'i tshad dpag tu med pa/ ye shes rin po che sna tshogs kyi phreng ba dang / chun 'phyang dang / shar bu'i rgyan dang / gzugs sna tshogs dang / sgra sna tshogs dang / dri sna tshogs dang / ro sna tshogs dang / reg bya sna tshogs kyis phyogs bcur 'khrigs par rang byung la/ mi sgrib par gsal ba'i rgyan bsam gyis mi khyab pas bklubs pa/ rnam par thar pa bzhi'i sgo nas 'jug pa'i sgo khyud can/ rnam par thar ba brgyad kyi rta babs dang ldan pa'i phyi dang nang med par kun du yang nang du gyur pa na mi 'jigs pa seng ge'i khri dang / stobs kyi glang po'i khri dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi rta'i khri dang / dbang gi rma bya'i khri dang / thogs pa med pa nam mkha' lding gi khri dang / rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal ba nyi zla'i dkyil 'khor dang // gos pa med pa pad+ma rin po che'i gdan la sku mdun dang rgyab med pa thams cad du yang zhal thal le bar gsal zhing // mtshan dang dpe byad du ldan pa/ bsam gyis mi khyab pa thams cad du sku gsung thugs sna tshogs par kun du snang ba/ lhun gyis grub pa'i sku gsung thugs chen po las thabs dang shes rab kyi zhabs gnyis mnyam pa'i brtul zhugs kyi skyil mo krung du bzhugs pa/ ye shes drug gi phyag // ye shes rin po che'i phyag 'bar ba can/ sku gsung thugs bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i dbu gsum dang ldan pa 'di lta ste/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par shes pa'i rgyal po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa gzugs kyi rgyal po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa tshor ba'i rgyal po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa 'du shes kyi rgyal po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa 'du byed kyi rgyal po dang / de dag kun kyang mthing ga dang / dkar po dang / ser po dang / le brgan dang / ljang gu'i mdog tu 'tsher ba/ btsun mo dam pa'i snang ba'i dbyings dang / sra ba'i dbyings dang / mnyen pa'i dbyings dang / dro ba'i dbyings dang / bskyod pa'i dbyings la sogs pa/ btsun mo'i tshogs dang gnyis su med pa'i chos kyis dbyings kun du mtha' yas par khyab pa ni 'di lta ste/ dper na til gyi gang bu bzhin du gang nas khyab par bzhugs so// de nas byang chub chen po rdo rje mthong ba dang / byang chub chen po rdo rje thos pa dang // byang chub chen po rdo rje snom pa dang / byang chub chen po rdo rje myong ba dang / btsun mo mthong bar bya ba dang / mnyan par bya ba dang / bsnam par bya ba dang / myang bar bya ba'i tshogs dang / byang chub chen po rdo rje mthong byed dang / byang chub chen po rdo rje thos byed dang / byang chub chen po rdo rje snom byed dang / byang chub chen po rdo rje myong byed dang / btsun mo 'das pa dang / da ltar 'byung ba dang / ma byon pa'i tshogs dang / 'joms pa chen mo reg pa dang / 'joms pa chen mo reg byed dang / 'joms pa chen mo reg shes dang / btsun mo rtag par ma yin pa dang / chad par ma yin pa dang / bdag tu ma yin pa dang / mtshan mar ma yin pa la sogs pa de lta bu'i tshogs brjod kyis mi lang ba dang gnyis su med par bzhugs so// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa btsun mo'i tshogs dang gnyis su med pa'i dkyil 'khor de dag nyid kyi gsang ba 'di nyid sku dang / gsung dang / thugs dang / yon tan phrin las rdo rje las phyung ngo // e/ e/ e ma'o// de bzhin nyid kyi dbyings nyid dang / dbang sgyur ye shes dkyil 'khor thugs dang rang snang ba nyid ting nge 'dzin gzugs brnyan sgyu ma rnam dag gsal ba ni sku dang gsung dang thugs yon tan phrin las sel med pa'i yid bzhin nor bu rin po che mi zad par ldan pa rgyan gyi 'khor lo rdo rje mchog gi gnas nyid do zhes rdo rje gsang ba'i tshig tu'o// gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid nges pa las gleng gzhi'i le'u ste dang po'o// // de nas bcom ldan 'das byed pa po rdo rje yid kun du bzang po thams cad ma lus pa'i rang bzhin gyi tshul rdo rjes btsun mo chos bya ba mo kun du bzang mo la 'jug par gyur te ched du brjod pa 'di brjod do// o~M chos kyi chos nyid shes bya'i dbyings// kun du bzang mo bde ba'i yum// ma g.yos rang bzhin dkyil 'khor ni// bdag yin bdag gi spyod yul ba// phyag rgya sna tshogs so sor gsal// nub phyogs 'og min gnas mchog tu// ma chags pad+ma'i gdan bting ba// dus gsum rgyal ba bzhugs pa'i gnas// rnam par thar pa'i sgo bzhi la// phyag rgya bzhi dang yang dag ldan// dbang dang skal min gsal ba'i phyir// nang dang phyi rim lcags dang ldan// rgyal ba yongs kyi sbas pa yi// sus kyang gting dpag dka' ba de// kun du bzang po nyid kyis gzigs// zhes brjod pas btsun mo bya ba mo chos kun du bzang mo la 'jug par gyur to// zhugs nas btsun mo bya ba mo chos kun du bzang mos bcom ldan 'das yid kun du bzang po dang / gnyis su med pa'i longs spyod bde ba la mnyam par gnas te ched du brjod pa brjod do// sems kyi sems nyid byed pa'i gtso// kun du bzang po rdo rje yid// ye shes drug gi rang bzhin te// shar phyogs mngon dga'i bsam yas na// nI la lta bu'i gter 'byin pa// gsang 'dus 'phrul gyi lde mig gis// rnam par thar pa'i sgo phye nas// byang chub mchog gis nang gtan dgrol// mnyam sbyor pad+ma'i gdan la bzhugs// 'gro don byang chub sems bskyed nas// 'gro lnga skye bzhi dbang du bsdus// sku gsung thugs gnas dbang bskur to// zhes brjod pas thams cad mnyam pa chen po'i tshul rdo rje nyid du gsal bar gyur to// zhugs pas phyogs bcu'i de bzhin gshegs pa ma lus pa thams cad gcig gi rang bzhin dbyer med pas de bzhin gshegs pa nyid de bzhin gshegs pa nyid la ched du brjod pa 'di brjod do// e ma'o rdo rje phung po'i yan lag ni// rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas lnga ru grags// skye mched khams rnams mang po kun// byang chub sems dpa'i dkyil 'khor nyid// sa chu spyan dang mA ma kI// me rlung gos dkar sgrol ma ste// nam mkha' dbyings kyi dbang phyug ma// srid gsum ye nas sangs rgyas shing // thams cad ma lus chos so cog // sangs rgyas nyid las gzhan pa min// sangs rgyas nyid las gzhan pa'i chos// sangs rgyas nyid kyis mi rnyed do// zhes brjod pas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mnyes par gyur to// de nas btsun mo bya ba mo chos kun du bzang mos bcom ldan 'das yid kun du bzang po dang gnyis su med par gyur nas ched du brjod pa 'di brjod do// e ma'o phyogs bcu'i stong khams ye shes dben// srid pa gsum nyid dag pa'i zhing // snyigs ma lnga nyid bde ldan nas// phung po lnga nyid mngon sangs rgyas// thams cad mchog gi snying po bas// gzhan du rgyal bas chos mi 'tshal// nyid las gzhan zhes bya ba'i chos// btsal kyang rgyal bas mi rnyed do// zhes brjod pas thams cad ye nas sangs rgyas par de bzhin gshegs pa nyid kyis mkhyen to// gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid nges pa las gleng bslang ba'i le'u ste gnyis pa'o// // de nas gnyis su med pa'i bdag nyid chen pos ye shes sangs rgyas pa'i sems ye shes su bskyed pa 'di gsungs so// e ma'o ngo mtshar rmad kyi chos// rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kun gyi gsang // skye ba med las thams cad skyes// skyes pa nyid na skye ba med// e ma'o ngo mtshar rmad kyi chos// rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kun gyi gsang // 'gag pa med las thams cad 'gag // 'gag pa nyid na 'gag pa med// e ma'o ngo mtshar rmad kyi chos// rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kun gyi gsang // gnas pa med las thams cad gnas// gnas pa nyid na gnas pa med// e ma'o ngo mtshar rmad kyi chos// rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kun gyi gsang // dmigs pa med las thams cad dmigs// dmigs pa nyid na dmigs pa med// e ma'o ngo mtshar rmad kyi chos// rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kun gyi gsang // 'gro 'ong med las 'gro dang 'ong // 'gro 'ong nyid na 'gro 'ong med// ces brjod pas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang btsun mo'i tshogs thams cad mnyes pas khyab par gyur to// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad btsun mo'i tshogs dang bcas pas ched du brjod pa 'di brjod do// e ma'o ye nas gsang ba'i chos// sna tshogs snang la rang bzhin gsang // ngo bo nyid kyis rab tu gsang // gzhan du min yang shin tu gsang // zhes brjod pas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad ye nas sangs rgyas pa'i ngo bo nyid du gcig pa'i mtshan nyid yin pas dbyer med na/ 'gro ba'i rnam par rtog pa ma rig pa la 'gro ba lnga'i rigs bsam gyis mi khyab par smin pa la thugs rje chen po'i sangs rgyas kyi ye shes chen po skyes nas ched du brjod pa 'di brjod do// e ma'o bde gshegs snying po las// rang gi rnam rtog las kyis sprul// sna tshogs lus dang longs spyod dang // gnas dang sdug bsngal la sogs pa// bdag dang bdag gis so sor 'dzin// sus kyang mi 'ching bcings med de// bcing bar bya ba yod ma yin// rnam rtog bdag tu 'dzin pa yin// nan gyis mkha' la mdud pa 'dor// bcings med rnam par grol med pa'i// ye nas lhun rdzogs sangs rgyas chos// bstan phyir spro ba sna tshogs mdzad// ces de bzhin gshegs pa nyid la ched du gleng ngo // gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid nges pa las don dam pa dang kun rdzob kyi byang chub kyi sems ye shes su bskyed pa'i le'u ste gsum pa'o// // de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad las thugs rje chen po byin gyis brlabs zhes bya ba'i rig pa'i skyes bu thub pa drug de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje las bton to// bton nas kyang las kyi dbang gis snrel zhi dang / yan man gyi 'jig rten drug gi phyogs bcu mtha' yas mu med pa'i stong gsum gyi stong chen po re rer thub pa chen po bcom ldan 'das re res 'dul ba rnam bzhis 'gro ba lnga'i don mdzad de bltams pa dang / rab tu 'byung ba dang / dka' thub mdzad pa dang / sangs rgyas pa dang / bdud btul ba dang / chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba dang / cho 'phrul chen po ston pa dang / mya ngan las 'das pa la sogs pa ston pa'i thub pa dus bzhi kun du mkhyen pa dang / thams cad kyi sems kyi rgyud du kun du mkhyen pa dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi spyan gyis kun du gzigs pa dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi snyan gyis kun du gsan pa dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi cho gas kun du don spyod pa dang / zag pa med pas kun du bzang po'i spyod pa rdzogs pa'i mngon par shes pa drug dang // kun du sku bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang / kun du thugs bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang / kun du zhal bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang / kun du gsung bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang ldan pa dang / bsam gyis mi khyab pa grangs med par yang phyogs bcur snang bar gyur to// de ltar snang bar gyur nas ji snyed pa'i thub pa chen po snying rje'i go 'phang chen po thams cad kyang 'di lta ste/ 'dul ba'i dbang gis lha dang mi'i theg pa dang / nyan thos kyi theg pa dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i theg pa dang / bla na med pa'i theg pas ma rig pa'i rnam par rtog pa nyon mongs pa stong phrag brgyad cu rtsa bzhi'i gnyen por chos kyi phung po stong phrag brgyad cu rtsa bzhi gsungs so// gsung ngo // gsung bar 'gyur ro// de dag thams cad kyang gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i phyi nang gi rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba 'dzin pa 'khrul pa la dgos pa dang / las dang las kyi 'bras bu chud mi za ba dang / las dang las kyi 'bras bus mi gos gos par mi 'gyur ba dang / gos pa med pa'i ston pa'i mthar thug go// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis// 'khor ba'i skyon dang / mya ngan las 'das pa'i yon tan bstan pa'i phyir de bzhin gshegs pa nyid la ched du brjod pa 'di brjod do// e ma'o dkyil 'khor bsam yas par// snying po bla med ji snyed pa'i// gzhan gyis mi 'phrogs rang bzhin rgyal// mtha' dang bral bas bdag med pa'o// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis ched du brjod pa 'di brjod do// e ma'o ji snyed 'jig rten 'khrul pa'i chos// ma rig rtog pa'i gzung 'dzin gyis// stong gi 'jig rten bsam yas par// phyi nang rten 'brel gnyis su 'khor// rtog pa'i bag chags stug po yin// mi mthun bde sdug myong bar 'gyur// de nyid ji bzhin dbyings nyid dang // rang bzhin bdag med tshul gcig ste// rang bzhin nyid la nyams pa med// yang dag sgyu ma'i tshul gnyis su// bdag dang bdag gi gzhan med de// de nyid ngo bo nyid dbyings pas// rnam dag dbyings nyid tshul gcig go// bdag dang bdag gi gzhan rnams ni// log par rtog pa tsam nyid las// phra zhing zab pa yod ma yin// log rtog nyid la nyid spyod de// gzhan du g.yo ba ci yang med// log rtog rgyu 'bras rgyun nyid kyang // gzhi rtsa med de skad cig ma// rnam par dag pa'i dbyings nyid tshul// nyid la dbang sgyur nyid spyod phyir// bdag dang gzhan dang rtog pa'i rgyun// rnam dag bla med theg pa'i mchog // theg pa bzhi yis nges 'byung la// theg pa gcig gi 'bras bur gnas// yang dag rtogs pas rab brtags na// rang bzhin med la cir yang 'grub// sangs rgyas mya ngan yong mi 'da'// chos kyang nub par mi 'gyur te// ma rig smin mdzad gdul ba'i phyir// 'byung gnas mya ngan 'da' bar ston// 'dul ba mdo sde chos mngon dang // dam tshig sgrub dang grub pa dang // sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi rgyud// ji snyed 'jig rten mtha' klas par// phyogs bcur kun du rab grags pa// gsang ba'i snying po las 'phros te// rang bzhin gsang ba'i snying po 'di// sde snod kun dang rgyud kun gyi// ston pa'i thub pa bsam yas pa// 'byung gnas gtan la nges par 'bebs// chos rnams ming du btags pa tsam// ston pa'i don dang mthun phyogs su// ming nyid tshig tu btags nas bstan// ston ming tshig la dngos po med// ces brjod pas chos thams cad ngo bo nyid kyis lhun gyis grub pa chen por gsal bar gyur to// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa lhun gyis grub pa gnyis su med pa'i dkyil 'khor de dag nyid kyi gsang ba 'di nyid sku gsung thugs dang yon tan phrin las rdo rje las phyung ngo // a'o srid rtse'i nyes dmigs bdag tu rtog las 'phros// rgyud drug skye 'gag lus dang longs spyod dang // gnas dang sdug bsngal 'khrul 'khor la sogs pa// log rtog nyid las gzhan du ci yang med// stong nyid bdag med ye mkhyen rang rig thugs// dmigs bya dmigs med med par dran dbang sgyur// ngo mtshar sku gsung yon tan zhing khams la// gzhan na med de de nyid de ltar yin// zhes rdo rje gsang ba'i tshig tu'o// thub pa drug gis sprul pa grangs med pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis gsungs pa yang de dag tu 'dus par de bzhin gshegs pa nyid kyis mkhyen to// gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid nges pa las chos thams cad gtan la phab pa'i le'u ste bzhi pa'o// // de nas de bzhin gshegs pa bcom ldan 'das dgyes pa chen pos 'gro ba thams cad kyi rang bzhin gyi dkyil 'khor yod par bstan pa dang / rigs rgyud drug tu yang bshad/ de la chos nyid kyi rigs ni thams cad kun la yang yod do// nam mkha' kyang kun la khyab par gnas so// de ltar chos kyi dbyings dang / nam mkhas kun la khyab kyang rnam par thar ba'i don ma rtogs na me long g.yas g.yogs pa dang 'dra ste gzugs brnyan snang ba'i bya ba byed mi nus so zhes gsungs nas yang 'di skad rdo rje 'chang gis gsungs so// mnyam nyid don rtogs rang rig rgyal po dang // rgya mtsho chen por chu klung 'bab pa ltar// bla med don rtogs thabs chen 'di dag tu// rnam pa'i theg pa bsam yas ma lus 'dus// a ho// bdag med gnyis rtogs pha rol phyin rdzogs pa// sa bcu rim gyis bsgoms pa'i rnal 'byor pa// sangs rgyas sar 'gro go 'phang thob pa'i lam// bden pa gnyis kyis rab tu thob par 'gyur// phyi nang rten 'brel sgyu ma mig yor tshul shes pa'i// dngos po gzugs la thogs med rab tu 'jug // dge bshes mi slob rang gi rig pas rtogs// byang chub sar 'gro yid bzhin bde ba'i mchog // bden bzhi don rtogs rab tu spong ba yi// ye shes bcu drug cha sbyangs rab zhi ba'i// rgyun zhugs la sogs rim par sbyangs nas ni// nyon mongs dgra rnams rab tu zhi ba'i sa ru 'gro// theg pa gang du bstan pa ma nges pa'i// yang na kun la mthun nas 'byam par 'jug // yang na nges med 'di zhes brtag tu med// 'di ni ma nges rdo rje 'chang gis gsungs// dge bcu spyod cing mi dge spong byed pa// 'dod khams lha dang mi ru skye ba'i rgyu// tshad med bzhi spyod mi g.yo sgom byed pa// tshangs gnas lha sogs skye ba'i rgyu yin no// chos kyi dbyings kyis kun la khyab gyur kyang // rang rig rtogs pa'i skal dang mi ldan na// ji ltar dmus long mdun du mdog bstan bzhin// 'di ni skal med rigs chad sa yin no// chos kyi dbyings kyis kun la khyab pa yis// bla med theg pa bsam yas gsungs pa yang // so so rang rig blo la snang bar zad// ngan song 'gro drug sna tshogs rgyu ba yang // 'khrul ba'i blo log rtog pa nyid snang ste// de bzhin nyid kyi dbyings la 'gyur ba med// mi dmigs rang rig goms byas bla na med pa'i mchog // log rtog bdag dang bdag gir 'dzin gyur na// dngos med mi sdug sna tshogs snang bar 'gyur// yang dag shes pa'i rang rig blo med na// bde gshegs zhing yang ngan song gnas su mthong // theg mchog mnyam pa'i don nyid rtogs pa ni// ngan song gnas nyid 'og min dga' ldan gnas// nam mkha'i dbyings ni de nyid bsam yas par// nyi zla gza' skar mtshan ma glog 'gyu dang // 'ja' tshon sprin mang sna tshogs 'khrugs gyur kyang // nam mkha'i dbyings la gyur cing nyams pa med// mi dmigs chos kyi dbyings ni bsam yas par// sku gsung yon tan phrin las rmad 'byung dang // 'jig rtog gtso mchog ma lus thams cad dang // 'khrul 'khor sdug bsngal sna tshogs rnam mang yang // de bzhin nyid la 'phel zhing bri ba med// ces rdo rje gsang ba'i tshig tu'o// rgyud kyi rgyal po sgyu 'phrul dra ba las thams cad la chos nyid kyi rgyu yod pa dang rigs rgyud chad pa dang rigs brgyad so sor dbye ba'i mdor bshad pa'i le'u ste lnga pa'o// // de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dgongs pa gcig tu gyur nas mnyam pa chen po'i tshul rdo rje'i dbyings su chos thams cad ye nas sangs rgyas pa'i ting nge 'dzin las mi g.yo bar chos thams cad ming tsam du gnas pa'i yi ge phreng ba 'khor lo zhes bya ba 'di sku gsung thugs rdo rje las phyung ngo // a rab tu brtan 'gyur a dkar las// shin tu phra ba'i a rnams spro// phyogs kun gang par gsal gyur nas// bsdus kyang 'phel 'grib med par brtan// de las ming tshogs gsal 'bar kun// spro zhing bsdu ba'ang de bzhin no// 'di ni rdo rje dngos grub kyi// brten 'byung ye shes rgyu yin no// a/ ka kha ga g+ha nga / tsa tsha dza dz+ha nya/ Ta Tha Da D+ha Na/ ta tha da d+ha na/ pa pha ba b+ha ma/ ya wa ra la/ sha Sha sa ha/ k+Sha/ i I/ u A/ e ai/ o au// 'di dag phyung bas 'jig rten drug gi phyogs bcu mtha' yas pa rnam pa drug tu g.yos// rab tu g.yos kun du g.yos nas chos thams cad ming gi mtshan nyid du gyur to// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis ched du brjod pa 'di brjod do// a ni stong dang mi stong gi// dbu ma dmigs su yod ma yin// thams cad ming tsam sangs rgyas kun// yi ge phreng ba nyid la gnas// a nyid sna tshogs par snang ba'i// ka la sogs pa bzhi bcu gnyis// sgra yi ming gis thams cad bsdus// mngon rdzogs rgyal por de nyid nges// e ma'o ngo mtshar ya mtshan gyi// 'phrul chen bzhi bcu rtsa lnga'i ming // tshig rnams ma lus 'dzin pa'i gnas// sna tshogs don kun smra zhing ston// dngos med yi ge rang bzhin sems// bdag med mtha' bral mi dmigs kyang // dbyibs dang kha dog ming tshogs kyis// rol pa cir yang sprul cing ston// phyogs bcu dus bzhi gshegs pa yi// ye shes sems dpa'i sku gsung thugs// dkyil 'khor bzhi bcu rtsa lnga nyid// yi ge mgo nas k+Sha la rdzogs// sems ni rang bzhin yi ge ste// yi ge dngos po yod ma yin// dmigs med de nyid sna tshogs pa'i// sku gsung thugs kyi 'khor lo che// sku gsung thugs ni ngo mtshar gyi// ya mtshan 'phrul chen rab 'gugs pa// dbyings la dbyings kyis bris pa ste// yi ge zhes ni de phyir brjod// mgo ni ma nor lam yin te// tshig ni shes rab ming du smras// shad ni thabs chen tshigs su gcod// a ni skye med de bzhin nyid// Tha ni sgyu 'phrul rdo rje nyid// Ta ni snang ba'i sgyu 'phrul nyid// Da ni sgyu 'phrul yid bzhin nyid// D+ha ni sgyu 'phrul rnam dag nyid// Na ni kun du sgyu 'phrul nyid// tha ni dra bas mngon rdzogs nyid// ta ni dra bas brtan pa nyid// da ni dra bas lham me nyid// d+ha ni dra bas 'khyil pa nyid// na ni dra bas kun du 'gyur// ka ni spyan gyi thugs kyi mchog // kha ni snyan gyi thugs kyi mchog // ga ni shangs kyi thugs kyi mchog // g+ha ni ljags kyi thugs kyi mchog // nga ni thugs kyang 'jig byed pa'o// tsa ni spyan gyi sku yi mchog // tsha ni snyan gyi sku yi mchog // dza ni shangs kyi sku yi mchog // dz+ha ni ljags kyi sku yi mchog // nya ni sku yang 'jig byed pa'o// pa ni spyan gyi gsung gi mchog // pha ni snyan gyi gsung mchog ste// ba ni shangs kyi gsung mchog yin// b+ha ni ljags kyi gsung gi mchog // ma ni gsung yang 'jig par byed// ya ni skye ba rnam par dag // wa ni gnas pa dag pa yin// ra ni 'jig pa dag pa ste// la ni stong pa dag pa'o// sha ni rtag med dag pa ste// Sha ni chad pa'ang yod ma yin// sa ni mtha' bral bdag med pa// ha ni mtshan ma med pa nyid// k+Sha ni ye shes thugs kyi thugs// i ni rdul snyed lha rnams su// I ni rdul snyed lha ma yin// u ni rdul snyed mi rnams su// U ni rdul snyed byol song rnams// e ni rdul snyed su// ai ni rdul snyed dmyal ba rnams// o ni thams cad 'jig par byed// au ni thams cad zhig pa yin// yi ge 'khor lo tshogs chen 'dis// sku gsung thugs kyi phreng ba bsdus// a ho// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa btsun mo'i tshogs dang gnyis su med pa'i dkyil 'khor de dag nyid mtshar ming tshogs bzhi bcu gnyis// 'dus ma byas nyid 'dus byas rdo rje dkyil 'khor 'byin pa'i dam// 'da' bar mi mdzad dbang med rgyu rkyen tshogs pa'i mthu chen yin// a ho// rdo rje gsang ba'i tshig tu'o zhes brjod pas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad yi ge 'khor lor gyur to// gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid nges pa las yi ge phreng ba 'khor lo bkod pa'i le'u ste drug pa'o// // de nas de bzhin gshegs pa rgyud kyi rgyal po sgyu 'phrul dra ba las shin tu gsang ba'i phyir gsang sngags kyi rgyud de'i phyi pa dang / nang pa thabs kyi rgyud gzhan la khams brgyad du bstan/ gtsug lag thams cad la yang khams brgyad du bstan pa yin/ lung gi spyi 'di ni shin tu zab pa'i phyir khams nyi shu rtsa gcig tu bstan te/ lung gi spyi yang rgyud dang gsung rab thams cad 'byung ba'i gnas yin// gsang ba'i dbang po dang gsang ba'i yul gnyis ka yang // skye mched dang khams thams cad 'byung ba'i gzhi yin pa'i phyir shin tu gsang bar gsungs so// dkyil 'khor de dag shin tu gsal bar bstan pa'i phyir nyid la nyid ched du brjod pa 'di brjod do// e ma'o ye nas gsang ba'i chos// thams cad kun la rang bzhin gnas// ngang gis dag mnyam ma rtogs pas// kun la yod cing rang bzhin gsang // gzhan du min la shin tu gsang // don nyid kyis ni gsang ba'i rgyu// mnyam pa'i rdo rje can gyis gsung // 'di ni byang chub snying po mchog // a ho// rdo rje gsang ba'i tshig tu'o// dbang po yul du snang ba'i rnams// byang sems ma yi// rdo rje gsang ba'i dbang por 'dus// rdo rje dbang po gsang ba'i thabs// dbang po yul nyid shes rab dbyings// dbang po'i thugs ni rdo rje sems// thams cad 'byung ba'i gter nyid dang // yas su// gsal ba'i thig le'i ngo bo nyid// hU~M o~M swa~M a~M ha~M rnams las// dkyil 'khor lnga dang khro phreng bsgom// phyogs bcu dus bzhi thams cad kyis// sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje che// dkyil 'khor kun gyi byed pa po// dkyil 'khor kun gyi sbyin pa spyod// slob dpon mnyes par ma byas shing // dbang rnams thob par ma byas par// nyan pa la sogs rtsom pa rnams// 'bras bu med cing brlag par 'gyur// dbu rgyan cod pan phreng ba dang // go cha rgyal mtshan phyag rgya dang // gdugs dang bum pa bza' btung dang // snying po lnga yis dbang bskur na// dus 'di phan chad rgyal ba'i sras// ngan song thams cad med pa dang // gnyen por gyur pa'i rtsal 'chang bas// tshe ring bde ba phun sum tshogs// kun du bzang po la sogs mtshan// mtho ris thar pa'i dbang por 'gyur// lus dang phung por bcas pa'i sa// rig 'dzin sa la gnas pa yin// rig 'dzin sa la gnas pa'i sa// bla med kun du bzang por 'gyur// yum dang sgeg mo la sogs la// de nyid byin gyis rlob par 'gyur// pho nya 'du 'phro mang po por 'gyur// zhes ched du brjod do// gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid nges pa las dbang sbyin pa'i le'u ste nyi shu gcig pa'o// de nas de bzhin gshegs pa dgyes pa chen po mnyam pa nyid la bzhugs nas lhag pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyis dngos grub myur bar len pa'i thabs 'di gsungs so// de bzhin nyid dang mnyam sbyor phyir// dam pa'i don gyis bsgom par bya// byang chub phyogs la gzung bar gnas// mchog tu bde ba'i zhing gnas pas// mnyam rdzogs chen po lhun bsgom zhing // byang chub sems su brtan par gzung // bya ba med las bya byed bya// mi gnas gnas la gnas par bsgom// b+ha ga'i dkyil du ling+ga a// mang yang // nam mkha'i dbyings su thams cad bsdus// thams cad mkhyen nyid bsam yas kyang // chos kyi dbyings su thams cad 'dus// thams cad yi ge hU~M du gyur// hU~M nyid gsang ba'i thugs rje'i dkyil// 'od zer 'phros pas 'bru gsum ste// yang na 'od zer 'bru lnga yi// lnga pa'i don spros bzhi bcu lnga'i// gzhan yang dkyil 'khor bsam yas mchog // ma bcos ngang gis gnas pa la// ye shes lhag pa'i dkyil 'khor bsgom// sen zlum zla ba gang ba yi// thugs kyi dkyil du gnas par bya// nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor gang ba yi// gzhal yas 'od zer 'bar ba'i khang // pad+ma'i gdan dang rin po che// de dkyil yi ge hU~M gnas pa// shin tu phra zhing yungs 'bru 'bar// gnas gcig dang ni gnas gsum dang // gnas lnga dag tu rab tu bsgom// shes rab spyan la 'dris pa dang // nr-i yi mig gis bltar yod par// shin tu phra zhing gsal bar bsgom// shin tu blo gsal 'dris gyur nas// phyogs bcu'i stong khams rdul snyed du// thugs rje'i byin brlabs bsam yas spro// spros kyang hU~M las nyams pa med// bsdus kyang phyogs rtag tu bsgom// gzhal yas khang dang gdan khri rnams// phra ba'i tshul de snga ma bzhin// mtshan dang dpe byad thams cad ldan// dbu rgyan yi ge lnga dang ldan// rdo rje 'khor lo ral gri 'bar// rin chen pad+ma dril bu 'bar// phyag rgya chen po de dag las// phyogs bcu ma lus gzhal yas khang // nyi zla gza' skar dkyil 'khor gdan dang rgyan// bde gshegs dkyil 'khor ma lus bsgom// thugs rje byin brlabs 'gro don mdzad// zhi ba phyogs gcig shes bya spro// sa bcu mnyam par sbyong byed cing // bde gshegs 'khor yang dag par byed// de ltar sgrub pa'i rigs mchog de// 'bras bu mngon du ma smin kyang // sdug bsngal thams cad yong mi 'byung // lha mi mtshan rdzogs yongs su 'grub// theg pa dman par yong mi skye// bde gshegs 'byung dang skol mi 'gyur// byang chub gzungs la zhugs pa yin// zhes nyid la nyid gsungs so// rdo rje gsang ba'i tshig tu'o// gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid nges pa las rdo rje sems dpa' sgrub pa'i le'u ste nyi shu gnyis pa'o// // de nas de bzhin gshegs pa dgyes pa chen nye bsnyen pa'i// sgrub pa dang ni sgrub chen po// yum gyi pad+ma'i dkyil 'khor du// bde ba'i thugs kyi dkyil 'khor spro// sangs rgyas sprin tshogs ma lus la// dgyes mnyam mchog gi sbyin pas bstim// 'dzegs nas bu dag 'gro bar byos// khong na gnas pa'i yang khong du// lcags kyi sgrom bu kha bsdam mo// dbyings nyid la ni nyid spyod phyir// dbyings nyid mchog gi gnas la spyod// de nyid mi gnas mya ngan 'das// rdo rje gsang ba'i tshig tu'o// gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid nges pa las gsang ba chen po man ngag gtan la phab pa'i le'u ste nyi shu drug pa'o// // de nas de bzhin gshegs pa dgyes pa chen pos mnyam pa'i dkyil 'khor la bzhugs nas nyid kyi sku la thams cad ma lus par ston te ched du brjod pa 'di brjod do// 'das dang da ltar ma 'ongs dang // 'byung bar ma nges dus 'di dag // snga phyi med par mnyam yin par// nges pa med par yang dag gsungs// 'jig rten 'das dang 'jig rten pa'i// rang dang spyi ru bstan pa dang // ji snyed brtan g.yo la sogs pa// sgyu ma mig yor tshul yin te// par sbyor// thabs dang thabs las byung ba yi// de ni byang chub rdo rje mchog // ji snyed brjod pa'i kha brgyud kyang // yang dag don gyi snying po ni// gang nas btsal kyang mi rnyed de// rang rig sgrib med dag pa yin// de la rtag 'grus goms pa ni// bsnyen pa'i dam pa de yin te// de ni ma nor lam yin par// a yis b+ho d+hi rab tu bsdus// de bzhin nyid kyi dbyings nyid ni// gcig gam 'di zhes bgegs rnams 'dul ba ni// phyogs bzhi dag gis gdul bar 'gyur// gal te de yis ma dul na// byang shar mtshams kyi bgegs 'dul ba// rdo rje rtse gsum nr-i mgo gdengs// i sha nyid kyang phyag na bsnams// 'byung po de kun rab tu btul// shar lho mtshams kyi bgegs 'dul ba// rdo rje ye shes me lce 'bar// me de nyid kyang 'tshig par byed// drang srong nyid kyang phyag rgyar bsnams// me lha gdon 'khor dbang du bsdus// lho nub mtshams kyi bgegs 'dul ba// rdo rje dang ni srin po'i mgo// rab tu rno ba'i ral gri 'bar// bden bral nyid kyang phyag na bsnams// srin po'i tshogs rnams dbang du bsdus// nub byang mtshams kyi bgegs 'dul ba// rlung gi ba dan nr-i mgo gdengs// shin tu drag po glang po'i brjid// tshig srung nyid kyang phyag na bsnams// g.yeng ba thams cad dbang du bsdus// 'og tu 'jig rten bgegs 'dul phyir// phyag rgya ri rab chen po ste// phag chen po ni phyag na bsnams// 'og gi bgegs rnams 'dul ba'o// gzhan yang nyi zla'i dkyil 'khor gyis// tsha dang grang ba'i sdug bsngal sel// me yi dkyil 'khor chen po yis// thams cad ma lus sreg par byed// chu yi dkyil 'khor chen po yis// thams cad ma lus 'khru bar byed// rlung gi dkyil 'khor chen po yis// thams cad ma lus gtor bar byed// gzhan yang ral gri 'khor lor bcas// mda' gzhu tho chen gri chen dang // rdo rje mdung chen dgra star bcas// mche gtsigs spu gri so dang ni// mda' dang mdung dang sti ra dang // gzhan yang phyag rgya sna tshogs so// dbus kyi he ru'i phyag rgya ni// sti ra dbyug to chen po dang // 'khor lo chen po rab tu 'bar// dung chen dmar gyis gang ba la// rdo rjes dkrug cing rab tu gsol// shar gyi khro bo'i phyag rgya ni// sti ra chen po'i dbyug pa dang // rdo rje chen po rab tu 'bar// nr-i mgo dmar chen bkang ba gsol// lho yi phyag rgya chen po ni// sti ra chen po'i dbyug pa dang // yid bzhin nor bu'i gzhal yas su// dmar gyi ar+g+ha rab tu gsol// nub kyi khro bo'i phyag rgya ni// sti ra chen po'i dbyug pa dang // pad+ma chags med rab tu 'bar// dung chen dmar gyis bkang ba gsol// byang gi khro bo'i phyag rgya ni// sti ra chen po'i dbyug pa dang // rdo rje rgya gram rab tu 'bar// dung chen dmar gyis bkang ba gsol// khro mo rnams kyang khro dang mthun// gnas dang yul gyi phyag rgya ni// rgyud gzhan dag dang mthun par bshad// ma mo rnams kyi phyag rgya ni// 'jig rten 'das mdo che las bshad// gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid nges pa sgyu 'phrul dra ba las phyag rgya spros pa'i le'u ste sum cu pa'o// // de nas bcom ldan 'das dgyes pa chen pos de dag gi dkyil 'khor bstan pa'i phyir ched du brjod pa 'di brjod do// 'bar ba'i dkyil 'khor rtsibs bzhi pa// gru chad bzhi yis rnam par brgyan// gru bzhi sgo khyud bzhi dang ldan// 'bar ba'i bar khyams gnyis kyis mdzes// thod sprul sna tshogs nyi mas brjid// 'bar ba'i 'phro ba mang po 'khrug // khyu mchog ma he gzig dang stag // gtum pa'i dom gyis sbar bas ni// dbang phyug lha chen la sogs bzung // smug gnag sngo gnag ser gnag dang // dmar gnag ljang gnag 'jigs pa'i sku// dbu gsum phyag drug zhabs bzhi bgrad// ko rlon gos ni sna tshogs gyon// rngam pa'i sgra chen 'jigs par sgrogs// sbrul dang thod phreng nyi zlar bcas// steng gi 'jig rten khor yug bcas// rdo rje dung chen gang ba dang // ral gri dgra sta gshol la sogs// rang gi lag cha sna tshogs bsnams// btsun mo 'dzin pa'i tshogs dang 'khril// gnas dang yul gyi phyag rgya dang // sgo bzhi phyag rgyar rab mdzes shing // slas dang byi mo tshogs kyi gtso// bcu gnyis dang ni brgyad kyis mdzes// rang gi stan dang lag cha dang // ci bgyi zhes te chas te gnas// zhes brjod pas 'jig rten drug gi phyogs bcu thams cad du 'bar ba'i dkyil 'khor kun du gsal bar gyur to// de nas dgyes pa chen po bcom ldan 'das nyid kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje sgyu 'phrul dra ba las rdo rje gsang ba'i tshig 'di phyung ngo // a ho// bskal par bcas shing dug tshogs 'bar ba yi// nyon mongs kun g.yo dkyil 'khor 'khor lo brjod dka' ba'i// ji snyed 'jig rten rgyan gyis rdul snyed bsam yas pa// ro tshogs khrag la brkam pa dpung gnyen kun bkye nas// zhen pa'i gdug mo shin tu gsal ba dka' ba yi// mi mngon dbyings nas gzugs kyi cho 'phrul bsam yas kyis// snyigs mar bcas shing mtshams sbyor kun ngam zil gyis gnon// rab tu gnon pa'i 'jigs byed bsam mi khyab// de bzhin de nyid gnyen por kun byung kun du gsal// ho/ chos rnams ji snyed 'gro drug smin byed brjod mi lang // dus mtha' rmongs la gnas pa brjod mi lang // 'dod pas zhen pa'i las kyang ji snyed ji srid par// drag po bdo ba'i rlung chen bsam mi khyab// bde bar bcas pa gzhan du med par brjod mi lang // bskal par bsags pa'i dug chen rab rtog kun du rtog // de rnams zil gnon khrag 'thung sku gsung 'jigs byed par// rkyen du bcas nas sbu bus 'bras bu smin pa rab smin ltar// dgyes pa chen po bcom ldan 'das ni mang po'i tshogs// dpag med bsam yas lhun grub pas// rab tu 'dul bar shin tu gsal// ho// khro bo'i rang bzhin gdug bar 'jigs pa ma yin zhing // zhi ba mdzes pa kun gyi yid dang 'thad par gnas rgyud yong ma yin / de nyid gnyis su mi pa'i cho 'phrul bsam yas thams cad kun du khyab// rigs lnga khrag 'thung 'jigs pa'i rol pa rdul snyed rab ston pa'i// rnam dag byang chub mchog gi dbyings te gsang ba'i snying por rab bstan nges pa nyid de shin tu gnas par gsal// ho/ rdo rje gsang ba'i tshig tu'o// gsang ba'i snying po de kho na nyid nges pa las khro bo'i dkyil 'khor bstan pa'i le'u ste sum cu gcig pa'o// // de nas bcom ldan 'das dgyes pa chen pos nyid kyi byin brlabs dang yon tan ston pa zhes bya ba 'di ched du brjod pa 'di brjod do// oM sangs rgyas rnal 'byor chen po ni// dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// ye shes snying po'i mchog nyid de// sangs rgyas kun du bzang po nyid// 'di yin gzhan na med pa ste// rol pa kun la mnga' brnyes shing // srid pa 'jig rten thams cad kun// sangs rgyas nyid de dus gsum du// ma g.yos lhun gnas snying po ste// rang bzhin che ba'i yon tan las// ma rtogs rmongs pa'i 'gro ba la// sgyu 'phrul dra bas mngon rdzogs pa// snying rje chags pa'i dam tshig gis// nga rgyal nyid kyi sku chen bstan// gdug cing gtum pa'i khams gsum na// 'dul ba'i zhing du rab sbyor zhing // phrin las rnam bzhi rdzogs par mdzad// ye shes ngo mtshar tsham ngam gyis// chos bzhi rnam dag che ba'i lta// ye shes sku ste khyad par che// chags pa'i tshogs kyis mtshan ma ni// 'dod chags chen po nyid kyi sku// gtum rngam gdug pas mtshan pas na// zhe sdang chen po nyid kyi sku// gdul bya zhing du rab sbyong zhing // chos nyid mnyam las bzhengs pas na// gti mug chen po nyid kyi sku// snod bcud dag pa'i spyod yul ba// thugs sku gsung las 'phros pa dang // rgyal ba nga yis mtshan pas na// nga rgyal chen po nyid kyi sku// gsang ba'i snying po bzhi bcu gnyis// thig le thugs su bsdus pa nyid// gzhan du me gtong shes rab phyag mtshan pa// gnyis med rig pa'i ye shes che// ming dang gzugs dang dbur gyur pa// phyag dang zhabs su rnam par brtags// brtags pa las ni 'phros pa'i sku// ci yang med las cing yang snang // skal bzang mchog gi sgyu 'phrul ba// dra ba'i dkyil 'khor rab tu rdzogs// brtags pa zig gnon chos nyid spyan// spyan ni chos nyid mnyam pa nyid// ji bzhin dbyings kyi yul la sbyor// rol pa'i rtsed mor sdang mig pa// gzhan du mi gzigs yul la gzigs// pad+ma 'khyil pa nyid sku gsung // mtshan mar 'dzin pa'i dngos po 'jig // ye shes chen po'i spyan bgrad las// khro gnyer glog stong 'gyur ba yi// me 'khor du gtogs pa mang nyung la// gdug pas zin par mi 'gyur cing // ljon pa lcug phran la sogs la// gdug pas gnas par mi 'gyur phyir// lnga pa zhes ni rab tu bsngags// bdag gis gdug par mchod pa'i su ro gcig phyir// sgyu ma rang bzhin mnar sems pa// dngos po thams cad 'jig rtogs na// sgyu mar snang ba thams cad kyang // chos kyi dbyings las mi gzhan te// mi dmigs pa nyid sgyu mar skyes// chos rnams thams cad rang bzhin ni// bdag srog gso ba'i rang bzhin med// snang ba thams cad chos kyi dbyings// mnar sems sgyu ma chos nyid do// thams cad mi dmigs de bzhin yin// kun kyang dbyer med chos phyag rgya// mi dmigs sgyu ma kun nas mnar// rtog pa kun nas mnar sems te// chos nyid sgyu ma mi dmigs te// chos nyid sgyu ma mi dmigs phyir// don dam kun rdzob ro gcig ste// ting nge 'dzin gyis dbang bsgyur na// thugs kyi phyag rgya chen po yin// mi dmigs kun nas mnar sems pa// 'dul ba'i bya ba bsam mi khyab// gsung gi phyag rgya chen po'o// zhe sdang spyi yi mtshan nyid ni// yang dag nyid kyis rab brtags na// rnam par byang ba'i mtshan nyid de// gnyis med zhe sdang spang du med// nga rgyal mtshan nyid bshad pa ni// khong nas 'gying zhing khengs sems pa// pha rol zil gyis gnon par byed// spyi yi mtshan nyid bshad pa ni// mi rtag sdug bsngal stong bdag med// nga rgyal spangs nas zhi bsgrub med// chos kyi dbyings su ro gcig pas// kun rdzob sgyu mar khong 'gying nyid// de bzhin nyid las mi gzhan te// chos nyid mi dmigs 'gying bar skyes// skye 'gying nyid na chos nyid de// 'gying ba'i rang bzhin mi dmigs dag // 'gying dang mi 'gying dbyer med phyir// chos sku phyag rgya chen po yin// mi dmigs pa nyid sgyu ma 'gying // 'gying bas zil gyis gnon pa nyid// chos kyi dbyings las mi gzhan te// sgyu ma chos nyid dbyer med phyir// don dam kun rdzob gnyi ga gcig // ting nge 'dzin gyis dbang sgyur na// thugs kyi phyag rgya chen po yin// mi dmigs sgyu mar 'gying ba ni// nga rgyal 'dul ba bsam mi khyab// gsung gi phyag rgya chen po yin// nga rgyal rang spyi'i mtshan nyid ni// rnam par byang ba'i mtshan nyid yin// zhi ba sgrub nga rgyal spang du med// 'dod chags rang spyi'i mtshan nyid ni// srid pa kun la zhen pa ste// spyi yi mtshan nyid bshad pa ni// mi rtag sdug bsngal stong bdag med// chags spangs ma chags bsgrub tu med// chos kyi dbyings su ro gcig phyir// kun rdzob sgyu ma'i rang bzhin du// 'dod cing chags pa sgyu ma sred// mi dmigs pa las mi gzhan phyir// mi dmigs de nyid sgyu mar skyes// chos rnams bdag las mi gzhan phyir// mi dmigs de nyid sgyu mar skyes// spyod pa sgyu ma ro gcig phyir// chos nyid chos can dmigs su med// rgyal ba kun dang dbyer med pa'i// chos kyi sku yi phyag rgya yin// mi dmigs sgyu mar 'dod cing chags// 'dod chags chos nyid mi dmigs te// sgyu ma mi dmigs dbyer med phyir// bden pa gnyi gar dbyer med gcig // ting nge 'dzin gyis dbang bsgyur na// thugs kyi phyag rgya chen po yin// mi dmigs dbyings nyid 'dod chags spros pa ni// 'dul ba bsam gyis mi khyab ste// gsung gi phyag rgya chen po yin// 'dod chags rang dang spyi yi mtshan// rnam par byang ba'i mtshan nyid yin// chags dang ma chags gnyis med pas// 'dod chags mtshan nyid spang du med// phrag dog kun gyi mtshan nyid ni// gzhan gyi phun sum tshogs pa la// sems dog rtog pa sgyu ma gzhan// thabs kyis sbyor ba sgyu ma'i rang bzhin can// phrag dog spyi mtshan bshad pa ni// mi rtag sdug bsngal stong bdag med// phrag dog spang zhing yangs bsgrub med// chos nyid du ni ro gcig phyir// kun rdzob sgyu ma gzhan gyi phun sum la// phrag dog rtog pa sgyu ma'i rang bzhin nyid// mi dmigs pa las mi gzhan te// mi dmigs pa nyid sgyu mar skyes// phun sum tshogs pa'i lhag par sbyor ba yi// thabs kyi rtogs pa sgyu ma'i chos nyid de// dus gsum rgyal ba kun dang dbyer med pas// chos sku phyag rgya chen po yin// mi dmigs sgyu ma gzhan gyi phun sum la// phrag dog rtog par 'dzin pa dang // rtog dang phrag dog mi dmigs te// sgyu ma mi dmigs dbyer med pa'i// bden pa gnyi gar ro gcig pas// ting nge 'dzin gyi dbang bsgyur na// thugs kyi phyag rgya chen po yin// mi dmigs gzhan gyi phun sum la// phrag dog rnam par spros pa ni// gdul ba'i bya ba bsam mi khyab// gsung gi phyag rgya chen po yin// phrag dog rang dang spyi bstan pa// rnam par byang ba'i mtshan nyid yin// dog pa spang zhing yangs bsgrub med// sems can rnam pa mang po kun// nang gi chen po lnga sogs bstan// rang spyi'i mtshan nyid bshad par bya// thabs dang shes rab ma rtogs pas// ma grol khams gsum 'khor ba yin// de ltar nges par ci mthong na// sngags kyis yongs su zin pa'i nad// kun la gnod par byed mi nus// de bzhin thabs dang shes rab rtogs// dug gsum sdug bsngal gnod mi 'gyur// thabs la mkhas pas ma zin na// lam gyi dge spyad stegs bcas kyang // mtho ris lha dang mi ru skyes// skye shi med pa'i sa mi thob// thabs mkhas snying rjes zin pa ni// mtshams med sems can ma lus kun// byang chub sems dpa'i snying rjes bsad// bsod nams dpag tu med pa thob// ma bsad na yang sems can yal bor te// snying rje med de sdig yod 'gyur// 'dod chags zhe sdang gti mug dang // nga rgyal phrag dog chen po dag // gang phyir byang chub sems de ni// rdo rje de bzhin gshegs par gsal// nyon mongs pa nyid de bzhin gshegs// ngo bo yin par gsal por gsungs// chos kun rang bzhin dag pa'i phyir// 'khor ba yongs su dag par 'gyur// thabs dang shes rab ldan pa la// nyon mongs thams cad byang chub rgyu// 'khor ba'i rang bzhin bdag med pas// de phyir de bzhin gshegs bsam yas// thabs dang shes rab ldan gyur pas// phyin ci log nyid byang chub lam// 'khor ba'i rang bzhin mi dmigs phyir// mya ngan 'das pa yod ma yin// gsang sngags bla na med pa yi// thabs kyis ji ltar zin bzhin 'grub// bsam gyis mi khyab nges pa med// don dam cir yang ma grub la// sgyu ma'i sprul pa bsam mi khyab// thabs chen dag gis zin pa ni// nyon mongs lam yang rnam par grol// thabs chen dag gis ma zin na// dge ba spyad kyang grol mi 'gyur// rnal 'byor don dam ldan pa yis// nyon mongs 'ching ba'i chos spyad kyang // rnam par grol bar 'gyur ba yin// 'khor ba dang ni mya ngan 'das// gnyi ga yod pa ma yin pas// 'khor ba yongs su shes pas na// de ni mya ngan 'das pa'i mtha'// nyon mongs phyin ci log rnams dag // thabs la mkhas pas zin 'gyur yang // grol la thar bar mi 'gyur na// byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis ni// 'dul ba'i dbang gis bya byed kun// rngon dang smad 'tshong ston pa'ang ltung // byang chub sems dpa'i spyod tshul bzang // phal la med pas mi rung na// sngags mchog shin tu zab pa yi// skye bo kun gyis bya bar 'byung // bdud rtsi dang du blang bar gsungs// mnyam dang mi mnyam dbyer med na// sku gsung rdo rje dbang thob 'gyur// grub pa'i rdzas su de phyir gsungs// shes rab mnyam pa ma rtogs na// byol song la la chos dang ldan 'gyur yang // drang srong 'tsho dang rtag mthun dang // ji srid 'tsho yi bar du 'dod pa spong byed pa// de dag grol bar ngas ma bshad// chos rnams thams cad yongs su dag pa yi// rnam bzhi tshul gyis don rtogs mngon// rgyu rnams rang bzhin dag pa dang // 'bras bu yongs su dag 'gyur te// rgyu yi mtshan nyid rnam par dag // phyi rol chen po lnga rnams te// sems nyid gzung 'dzin gnyis snang ba// gzung ba'i yul nyid 'byung ba che// rgyud nyid rang gi sems yin pas// 'byung ba chen po rgyu las dag // 'bras bu yongs su dag pa ni// sems can kun gyi rus pa ste// rdo rje byang chub sems yin te// sha ni pad+ma rak+ta yin// dri chen dri chu gur gum chu// so so'i lus la gnas pas dag // don dam dmigs med dag pas ni// phyi nang chos rnams thams cad kyang // gang gi ngo bo ma yin te// skye 'gag med pas ye nas dag // kun rdzob ye nas dag pa ni// sgyu ma'i rang bzhin thams cad snang // chu zla'i tshul du mi dmigs gnas// mi dmigs pa nyid sna tshogs snang // de bzhin gshegs par ye nas mnyam// de bas gtsang sme med par spyod// sems can rtog pa bzlog phyir sman// gtso ru dang du blang bar bya// de bas sems can phyin ci log // chos rnams thams cad dag par ma shes te// thabs dang shes rab don ma rtogs// kha cig gis ni 'tsho ba'i bar du zos// kha cig gis ni drang srong ji bzhin du// sha spangs rtswa dang chu la zos// zos kyang ma grub don ma rtogs// rnal 'byor thabs ldan rnams kyis ni// rang bzhin yongs kyis dag pa'i phyir// mnyam pa'i dbyings kyis rab rtogs pas// thabs dang shes rab 'brel pa yi// the tshom med par 'grub par 'gyur// dngos dang dngos med rtogs pa mtshan// gtsang dang mi gtsang rtogs pa mtshan// mtshan ma nyid kyang rnam spangs te// mkhyen pas dbul la gnas mi 'gyur// bsgrub pa'i rdzas su yang dag gsungs// byang chub sems dang sha chen dang // dri chen dri chu rak+ta dag // sgrub pa pos ni nan tan bya// dngos grub ya mtshan chen po 'grub// tshe la dbang dang rig pa 'dzin// mkha' la 'phyo dang thogs med 'grub// mthar ni skye med rdo rje yis// gzhan yang ji ltar dmigs pa bzhin// 'grub 'gyur 'di la the tshom med// gsang ba'i snying po'i don nyid kyis// yi dam mi spang rtag bsgom zhing // ye nas lha yi mtshan nyid ni// dus gsum gshegs pa thams cad kyi// lha spangs dge spyad don med 'gyur// lha ni mi spang don nyid ni// lhun grub ye shes thams cad kyi// bdag dang gnyis med so so ma yin pa'i// dus gsum bder gshegs dkyil 'khor thams cad kyi// sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje bdag po ste// yongs su rdzogs par bsgom pa'i don// dkon mchog gsum spangs tshangs par spyad pa'i don med 'gyur// bdag nyid lha dang mnyam sbyor na// yon tan chung yang 'grub par 'gyur// ye nas mnyam nyid sbyor nas su// lha nyid du ni rtag tu bsgom// bder gshegs kun dang mnyam par 'gyur// sku gsung ye shes lnga rdzogs grub// rdo rje slob dpon smad mi bya// byang chub ston pa 'dren pa po// long ba dmigs bu 'dren dang 'dra// nyon mongs sdug bsngal mtsho skems yin// slob dpon de la smod pa ni// dper na na mun khung sgron bsad na// mthong ba'i don ni mi rtogs bzhin// sdug bsngal nyam thag yun // bskal pa mang por myong bar mngon// de bas de la gus pa rtag tu gyis// lus la dbang ba'i rgyal po bas// shin tu gtso bor blang bar bya// drin chags bskyed pa'i pha ma bas// shin tu lhag pa'i ri mo bya// rdo rje mched dang lcam dral ni// bla med byang chub zhing 'gro ba'i// chos nyid dam tshig smon lam mthus// byang chub rin chen sar nges pas// de la ldog cing 'khu ba ni// rang la rang gis mtshon btab na// rang srog tshe rabs lnga brgya'i bar// rang gis srog gcod phung bar 'gyur// tshe 'di mi bde sna tshogs pa// mi bde bzhin du 'byung bar 'gyur// 'jig rten pha rol dag tu yang // ngan song gsum dang mi khom pa'i// sdug bsngal kha brgyud myong bar 'gyur// yun ring rtag tu mi thar ba'i// shin tu nyam thag myong bar 'gyur// grub pa gcig bzhin lhan cig spyod// gnyis med dad pas rjes spyod spun// bder gshegs dkyil 'khor bla med yin// shes rab gsal bas rtag tu gdung // zhes gsungs/ gsang ba gzhan la mi bsgrags shing // sku gsung thugs kyi dam tshig rnams// rnal 'byor mnyam pa rnam gnyis kyis// thabs gsungs// thabs la mkhas pas byas pa yin// gsang sngags skyon yod ma yin te// thugs rje chen po thabs mkhas kyis// snod ma yin dang blo rtul rnams// las 'phro ngan pa'i don phyir gsang // brgya la gang zhig gsang don 'di// las 'phro ngan la bsgrags 'gyur na// dper na gtsub shing mes gtsubs nas// gtsub shing nyid kyang 'tshig par snang // gzhan yang tshig par gyur pa bzhin// chos don bzang po me dang 'dra// skal ba chung zhing shes rab dman// blo ngan rgyu 'bras rmongs pa rnams// mnyam pa nyid la skur 'debs pas// ngan song gsum du 'phangs par 'gyur// gsang don ma rtogs sdug bsngal rmyong 'gyur te nyes skyon med// ces gsang ba'i tshig tu'o// dam tshig sum brgya pa rtsa ba bco lnga mdo bshad pa'i le'u ste drug cu brgyad pa'o// // de nas de bzhin gshegs pa dgyes pa chen pos bzhugs gnas dang / bo bdud rtsi 'khyil pa yi// dzaHhU~M ba~M hos dgug par bya// bdag dang khro bo gnyis med par// yang nas yang du bsgrub par bya// sku rnams gsal bar gyur pa dang // zhing chen 'og tu gzhug par bya// bsgom par bya// pho nya mang pos nr-i bkug nas// zhing la yang nas yang du gzhug // snar dang ser dang mdog snum 'byung // de nas bdud rtsi'i ting 'dzin gyis// lan grangs 'bum phrag mang por ni// bskul bar bya// de nas yi ge 'bru lnga dgod// gsal zhing 'tsher bar bsgom par bya// dbang po lnga dang dbang po'i tshul// yan lag lnga la rigs lnga'i tshul// rdo rje ting 'dzin de yis bsgom// de nas zhing de 'gul 'gyur nas// zhing de drag tu 'gul ba dang // shin tu zhags pas bsdam par bya// yan lag rnams kyang gzhum par bya// phyogs bzhi dag tu thod pa bstan// ha ya grI ba'i skur bsgoms shing // sngags ni 'bum phrag mang du bzlas// phyogs bcur spro zhing zhing la bstim// de nas zhing de drag 'gul nas// rdo rje ting 'dzin de yis ni// brtan pa nyid du bsgom par bya// de nas par par byed pa dang // a nr-i bri du gang yin pa// rdo rje drag tu bdeg cing dbab// thod pa'i kha nas nr-i phyung nas// rdo rje ting 'dzin so yis gcad// rdo rje sngags zos khong du bstim// gnyis su med par bsgom par gsungs so// dang por de bzhin nyid du gsal zhing 'dris par bsgom// de nas bdag gi snying gar a gsal zhing 'tsher ba gcig bsgom mo// a de shin tu gsal bar gyur pa dang / phyogs bcur 'od du 'phros par bsgom/ 'od de slar a la bsdu zhing bstim/ ma dang a las nyi ma dang zla ba'i dkyil 'khor bstim zhing 'tsher la gsal bar bsgom/ hrI las pad+ma'i dkyil 'khor gsal bar bsgom/ hU~M shin tu 'od 'bar bar bsgom/ snying gi dkyil 'khor du rdo rje sems dpa' mtshon gang ba gcig phyag rgya dang bcas par bsgom/ bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis kyi sngags dang / yig 'bru dang / phyag rgya yang gsal bar bzlas/ 'bru gsum dang 'bru lnga yang bzlas/ 'dug 'bru bzhis mtshams gcad/ rtag tu hom bya/ tshogs dang mchod pa yang bya/ mang po mi nus pa'i don du hom gang bgyi yang rung // dkyil 'khor gyi dbus kyi gtso bor spyi ni rdo rje sems dpa'/ drag po yang rdo rje/ dbang pad+ma he ru ka/ rgyas pa rat+na he ru ka/ zhi ba bud+d+ha he ru ka/ spyan drang ba ni e h+ye hi ma hA kA ru NI ka zhes hom gang byed pa'i lha gtso bo nas spyan drang // mchod pa dang ar+g+ha dbul ba ni drag po'i mgor ni/ sngags ril hU~M/ zhi ba la mgor ril a~M/ bar ma rnams la yang de bzhin sbyar// spyan drang ba ni gang mdzad pa'i gtso bo nas zhi la shAn+tiM bsnan/ spyi ni la so so rang sngags rdzogs/ drag po lho/ dbang nub/ rgyas pa byang // zhi ba shar/ spyi gang yang rung gru gsum dang thod pa kha gdangs so// zla gam dang / pad+ma dang / chags med de/ phyag rgya rnam pa bdun la phyag rgya chen po dang / chos nyid kyi phyag rgya dang / dam tshig gi phyag rgya dang / las kyi phyag rgya dang / thabs dang / shes rab kyi phyag rgya dang / ting nge 'dzin gyi phyag rgya dang / lhag pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi phyag rgya'o// rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po sgyu 'phrul dra ba las hom rnam bzhi'i le'u ste bdun cu bzhi pa'o// // de nas de bzhin gshegs pa rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po sgyu 'phrul dra ba las/ rmad du byung ba'i dam tshig bco lnga mdo 'di ltar yang bshad de/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyis// thams cad mnyam pa'i ngang nyid du// dbyings su ro gcig de bsdus te// don du mi 'gyur yong ma gsungs// yon tan mchog gi 'dod pa ni// snang srid ma lus thams cad kun// mnyam pa'i zhing du sbyor bas na// chags pa med pa'i tshul du spyod// 'di ni rnam dag legs pa'i lam// byang chub mchog tu 'gro ba'i gnas// bde chen mi zad gter du 'gyur// cis kyang mi tshugs rdo rje'i sku// nyon mongs sdug bsngal 'dod chags ni// lus dang zas kyis bsgribs 'gyur te// gnas nas gnas su 'gro// skom dang bkres pas nyon mongs 'gyur// rnag khrag ngan skyugs rtag tu mthong // bde la spyod pa'i dbang yang med// rtsub cing gdug pas bsrung bar 'gyur// thugs rje chen po'i zhe sdang ni// 'khor ba'i mya ngan sgo bcad cing // bder gshegs lam du 'dzud par byed// yang dag don dang ldan par 'gyur// thugs rje tshul gyis khro ston zhing // shin tu mnyam pa'i ngang du 'jog // rdo rje sems dpa'i zhi ba yis// yang dag mchog gi bde ba 'grub// ye shes gsal ba'i bde ba ni// bdag dang bdag gi dbyer med de// rang bzhin med pa'i dbyings su rol// thams cad brjod du med pa'i ngang // kun du khyab pa'i sku mnga' ba// shin tu 'od gsal rnam dag lam// byang chub sems dpa'i sgrib pa sbyong // sems can nyon mongs dug sel 'gyur// thams cad zhing sbyong nga rgyal ni// yon tan bskyed pa'i mdzod yin te// nga med bdag med mi dmigs la// su zhig de la nga rgyal skyed// dpung bzhi'i tshogs kyis mi thub pa'i// shin tu rgyal ba'i khyu mchog 'grub// lha srin bdud sde tshar bcad pa'i// dpa' bar 'gro ba'i ting 'dzin thob// phrag dog yangs pa'i don sbyor ba// nga dang bdag med don rtogs na// dog dang yangs pa gnyis med de// bde mchog dkyil 'khor yangs pa 'grub// phrag dog dngos po mi shes shing // nga dang bdag tu 'dzin 'gyur na// lha ma yin gyi gnas su skye// de nas gnas su 'gro// gal te yul sa rnyed gyur na// shin tu mi bde dog par 'gyur// gzhan yang longs spyod thams cad la// dbang byar med cing gzhan dbang 'gyur// mdor na nyon mongs sdug bsngal 'grub// phrag dog yang dag rtogs pa ni// nga dang bdag tu 'dzin pa dang // phyin ci log la phrag dog ste// thams cad gnyis su med par sbyor// bde ba mchog kyang 'grub par 'gyur// gnyis med don yang rtogs par 'grub// nga med bdag med dbyings su thim// lhun grub don mchog 'grub par 'gyur// yid la lha ni rtag bsgoms na// rgyu 'bras lhun gyis grub pa yi// bdag gis kun du dbang bsgyur te// rig 'dzin gnas su skye bar 'gyur// rdo rje'i rigs kyis bsgrub bya ba// sgrol dang sbyor bas mthar phyin 'gyur// sbyor ba nyid ni sgrol ba yin// rang bzhin gyis ni sbyor sgrol dang // sgrol ba nyid na sbyor ba yin// ting nge 'dzin gyis sbyor sgrol dang // dbang po'i yul dus sbyor sgrol dang // thabs chen dag gi sbyor sgrol dang // mngon du phyung ba'i sbyor sgrol lo// yang na sbyor sgrol bdag la sogs// shes rab dbyings dang bdag tu sbyor// thabs chen sprul pa bsam mi khyab// dbyings dang dbyings su thams cad sgrol// rol pa'i phrin las bsam mi khyab// thugs rje sprul pa bsam mi khyab// sbyor sgrol phrin las bdag la rdzogs// byang chub sems sprul phyogs bcur 'phro// ngan song gnas rnams stongs par byed// rig 'dzin bde ldan thob par byed// bla med zhing rnams dag par byed// sku gsung lhun grub phyogs bcur 'dul// rdo rje zhes ni mtshan bsgrags te// theg dman rnams kyang rdo rjer dgod// zad mi shes pa'i gter yang 'grub// rdo rje rig pa 'dzin pa'i sku// thams cad dbyer med mnyam pa'i sku// thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes mchog // thugs rje sprul pa dpag med kyis// 'gro drug dus gnas ma lus mkhyen// 'gro ba nyid na nyid kyi sku// nyon mongs byang chub lam du mkhyen// 'khor ba nyid ni bde gnas so// chos kyi dbyings dang sems can mtha'// dbyer med yang dag nyid du'o// rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po sgyu 'phrul dra ba las rmad du byung ba'i dam tshig bco lnga 'di ltar yang bshad pa'i le'u ste bdun cu lnga pa'o// // de nas de bzhin gshegs pa rgyud kyi rgyal po/ sgyu 'phrul dra ba las dam tshig rnam par spros pa 'di nyid la nyid ched du brjod pa 'di brjod do// spros pa rdo rje zhes bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ zhe sdang rdo rje'i thugs rje'i ngang // dmyal ba'i gnas rnams tshar gcod pa'i// brgyad gnyis bcu drug zhing du sbyor// tsha ba rnams la bsil ba'i sman// grang ba rnams la dro ba'i sman// bsil dro 'jam rtsub cha snyoms pa// thugs rje'i byin rlabs de ltar ston// byin rlabs ya mtshan rmad po che// chags pa'i ye shes zhes bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ chags pa med pa'i tshul gyis ni// 'dod pa kun la longs spyod bya// ji ltar bde ba'i ro myong zhing // myong tshor nyid na rang bzhin med// chags pa med pa'i ye shes kyis// gnas rnams tshar gcod cing // lus dang zas kyis bsgribs pa yi// nyon mongs gnyi ga med par ston// gti mug ces bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ nga dang bdag med gnyis med pa'i// shes rab chen po'i 'od gsal gyis// dran smra med pa'i sdug bsngal bsal// rmongs med sgrib pa dag par byas// ye shes gsal ba'i thugs rje yis// bya byed med par nyon mongs sgrol// byol song gnas ni stongs byed cing // thugs rje'i sgron ma de ltar sgron// phrag dog ces bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ yangs pa chen po'i ye shes kyis// nga dang bdag 'dzin rnams la ni// thugs rjes gnyis med mnyam sbyor zhing // dog dang yangs pa gnyi ga med// rgya chen yangs pa'i blo ldan pas// 'di la mi chud gang yang med// thams cad yangs pa nyid du sbyor// lha ma yin rnams stongs par byed// nga rgyal bde mchog ces bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ ye nas chos nyid mnyam pa la// nga dang khyod ces bya ba med// thams cad dbyings su ro gcig ste// gnyis med mtshan nyid bsnan du med// che chung med pa'i ngang yin pas// bya ba dag ni med par bstan// nga rgyal bdag med rtogs pa yis// dregs pa'i gnas rnams stongs par byed// rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal ba zhes bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ 'jig rten 'di na ci yod pa// ming dang tha snyad 'dzin pa dag // so so'i mtshan nyid gzhig byas na// rang bzhin med de yang dag nyid// rang byung chen po'i ye shes kyis// thams cad sangs rgyas zhing du sbyor// ma bcos ma byas ngang gis gsal// ye nas 'od gsal sangs rgyas zhing // nyid kyi dkyil 'khor zhes bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ rang bzhin nyid la gnas pa yi// sus kyang ma byas rang byung ste// thams cad de bzhin nyid du sbyor// gnyis med dbyings kyi ngang du thim// rang byung ye shes dkyil 'khor gyis// ma lus de bzhin nyid du sdud// sdud dang mi sdud gnyi ga med// yang dag kho na nyid du'o// bde ba'i ngang nyid ces bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ thams cad ma lus rnam par dag // nyid kyi dbyings las mi gzhan phyir// bde dang mi bde gnyis ka med// thams cad dbyings su ro gcig ste// ji bzhin nyid kyi ngang btsan par// yang dag nyid kyis de skad gsungs// bshad dang nyan pa'ang gnyi ga med// de bzhin nyid du gnyi ga 'du// dus bzhi rgyal mchog ces bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ gong na med pa'i ye shes mchog // thams cad kun la dbang bsgyur te// thams cad mnyam pa nyid du sbyor// 'das dang ma 'das thams cad dang // 'byung dang 'byung bar ma nges pa'i// ye shes rtogs pa'i khyad par gyis// dus bzhi snga phyi med pa yi// mnyam pa nyid du lhan ner sbyor// lhun grub ces bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ 'jig rten 'das dang 'jig rten pa'i// thams cad dbyer med byang chub ste// ye nas rnam par dag pa'i chos// ma bcos lhun gyis grub pa yi// byang chub lam chen 'di yin te// thams cad dbyer med nyid du 'dus// byang chub don sgrub ye nas rdzogs// mnyam pa'i zhing du thams cad thim// rdo rje skye gnas zhes bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ theg pa che mchog rigs su nges// rigs te byang chub bstan pas gzung // thams cad mnyam pa'i dbyings shes na// rigs mchog kun gyi skye gnas yin// skyes pa nyid na skyes pa med// las dang las kyi bag chags med// cis kyang ma gos thams cad 'joms// skye shi med pa'i sa yang yin// byang chub kyi zhing bkod pa'i dam tshig ces bya ba ni/ phyogs bcu mtha' yas mu med pa'i// snang grags bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i// phyi dang nang gi gnas pa dag // de bzhin nyid kyi dbyings su thim// mdor na zhing khams ma lus par// yon tan rin chen bkod pa yi// ye shes rgyan gyis spros pa rnams// zhing de yon tan bsam mi khyab// ye shes bzhugs gnas zhes bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ gzung 'dzin bral ba'i ye shes ni// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi gnas// gsang sngags chen po grub 'dod pas// gzung 'dzin bral ba'i ye shes thob// chos kyi dbyings dang sems can ni// gnyis med de bzhin nyid du gcig // de ltar rtogs pa'i skyes bu ni// rdo rje bzhugs gnas yin par bshad// mi 'jigs pa'i rgyal mchog ces bya ba'i dam tshig ni// rnam par byang dang nyon mongs gnyis// so so yod pa ma yin te// nyon mongs gnyen pos bcos su med// thams cad dbyings su ro gcig pas// de la 'jigs pa'i gnyen po med// cis kyang mi tshugs gong na med// mchog tu bde ba'i zhing yang yin// nga med bdag med rgyal ba'i mchog // gzhal yas khang brtan zhes bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ phyogs bcu dus bzhi thams cad kun// rgyal ba'i zhing du sbyor ba ni// dog yangs tshad kyang dpag tu med// sangs rgyas spyi gtsug lta bu'i mtshan// ye shes rgyu las grub pa'o// ji ltar dmigs pa bzhin du 'grub// zag pa zad las grub pa yi// nams kyang 'jigs med chos kyi dbyings// sna tshogs kun sbyor zhes bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ gdol pa can gyi chos min pas// ci ltar bsams pa bzhin du 'grub// rig pa rang dbang gyur pas na// stong par bya 'am mi stong bya// thams cad dbyer med ngang yin pas// kha dog dbyibs dang rin po che// thams cad khyab par yungs 'bru'i tshul// bsam yas mtha' dbus med pa'o// 'dren byed gnas stobs zhes bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ ma rig log rtog bsam yas kyis// 'jig rten khams rnams bsam yas pa// 'khor ba'i rgyu dang 'bras bu gnyis// gzhi rtsa med pa'i skad cig ma// yang dag byang chub sems rig na// ma rig rgyu 'bras rnam par dag // nyon mongs pa nyid byang chub ste// thams cad ma lus bde gnas so// lam lnga ston byed ces bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ ting 'dzin rnam gsum bsgom byas te// nyon mongs lam lnga'i sgo bkag nas// lam lngar snang ba rnam rtog yin// rtog dang mi rtog gnyi ga med// gnyis mar snang ba gnyis// sgyu ma yin pas rang bzhin mnyam// mnyam pa nyid na mi gnas pa'i// bsod nams ye shes tshogs rdzogs te// ye shes gnyis kyi dkyil 'khor la// theg mchog rdo rje ma lus rdzogs// dpe byad bzang po dpag tu med// thams cad dbang sgyur zhes bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ shin tu rtogs pa'i khyad par gyis// spyod yul thams cad smon na mkhyen// de bzhin nyid dang kun rtog la// gnyis su med pas dbang bsgyur te// ma lus thams cad bde ldan zhing // thams cad byang chub mchog tu 'gyur// ye nas dngos po med pa la// ji ltar dmigs pa bzhin du 'grub// rig 'dzin gnas stobs zhes bya ba'i dam tshig cad kun// bdag gi ngang du gnas pas na// bdag la bdag gis dbang bsgyur nas// spyod yul thams cad smon mi dgos// che mchog rnam dag ces bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ rig pa'i rgyal po rang gyur pas// thams cad kun la dbang bsgyur te// gong na med pa'i sa mnan pas// thams cad kun gyi gtso bo yin// thams cad ma lus gnyis med pas// bsgo dang bsgo bar bya ba min// de bzhin nyid la dbang bskur bas// thams cad dbyings su ro gcig go// chos thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor zhes bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ phyi nang snod bcud bdag rnams la// rang bzhin dkyil 'khor ye nas gnas// chen po'i gzugs snang thams cad ni// de bzhin gshegs pa'i dkyil 'khor nyid// sgyu ma'i rtsal rnams 'dzin 'gyur ba'i// de bzhin yum gyi dkyil 'khor ro// rang rig byang chub dkyil 'khor te// thams cad kun nas 'khyil bar gnas// zad med gter chen zhes bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ zag bcas gnod sbyin nor dang 'dra// sems can 'phel 'grib zad 'gyur gyi// de bzhin gshegs pa'i yon tan ni// zad med 'phel 'grib med pa yi// mang po spros pas 'phro mi 'gyur// nyung ngu bsdus pas sbom po min// zad med rin chen gter yin pas// thams cad kun la khyab pa'o// rnam dag byang chub ces bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ chos rnams ma lus thams cad kun// ye nas rnam par dag pa la// rnam rtog rkyen gyis glo bur du// khams gsum 'khor ba'i btson rar gnas// rang rig sgrib med dag pa yis// mya ngan 'das dang 'khor ba gnyis// rang bzhin med par don rtogs na// sangs rgyas zhing du rnam par dag // gzung 'dzin dril byed ces bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ phyin ci log tu rnam brtags na// bdag dang bdag gir so sor snang // de la 'dzin pa gnyis zhugs nas// rang bzhin med bzhin so sor snang // yang dag rtogs pas rab brtags na// dngos po thams cad stong pa yin// dngos dang dngos nyid mi gnas pa// de rtogs sdug bsngal bral byed yin// yum 'gyur dbyings phyug ma'i dam tshig ni/ 'byung ba lnga la brten 'gyur na// thams cad 'byung zhing ma lus gnas// skye 'khrungs ma lus gzhi yang yin// thams cad kun gyi rgyu yang yin// de bzhin shes rab rnam gsum gyis// le lo med pa'i brtson pa 'bod// de bzhin dbyings nyid rtogs gyur na// bla med byang chub 'byung ba'i gnas// chos la skyon med ces bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ bla na med pa'i dkyil 'khor dang // ngan song gnas rnams ma lus kun// rgyu nyid rang bzhin gnyi ga dag // rang bzhin ye shes de bzhin no// 'bras bu rnam par dag pa yi// 'jig rten brtan g.yo la sogs pa// snang ba nyid na ngo bo med// de nyid chos sku chen po yin// sems can don byed ces bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ byang chub sems su don gcig pas// rtsa ba snying rje chen po 'byung // thabs kyis pha rol phyin pa spyod// nyon mongs lam nas 'gro bar byed// nyon mongs khams gsum gnas pa yang // phyin ci log nyid snang ba yin// der rtogs mtho ris thar pa'o// rtogs nas don 'dzin ces bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ thams cad lhun gyis grub pa dang // sgyu ma mig yor tshul shes pa// gnyis ka rang rig nyid du 'dus// de nyid yang dag yin par bshad// sgra dang tshig tu brjod pa ni// yang dag don gyi snying po 'byin// ming tshig sgra la mi rten par// blo yi gting du go bar bya// sems la gnas bcas zhes bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ thams cad ma lus chos so cog // sems nyid las ni gzhan na med// sems dang chos su dbyer med pas// byang chub lam de ring ba min// gang nas ma 'ongs gar mi 'gro// rtog med rang rig kho na tsam// sangs rgyas sems can sems la gnas// brjod med spros med ces bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ 'jig rten 'das dang 'jig rten pa'i// sna tshogs ji snyed brjod pa yang // so so'i mtshan nyid ma gtogs pa// ba spu tsam yang brjod pa med// bsod nams chen pos bstangs pa yi// sangs rgyas zhing nyid dag pa'o// las ngan dag gis khams gsum gnas// de nyid dbyings las spros pa med// mi 'gyur rdo rje gsung zhes bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ rnam dag sku gsung sprul ba dang // che mchog sna tshogs bstan pa yang // byang chub sems la snang 'gyur te// snang ba nyid na dbyings su 'ub// phyin ci log g.yo bsam yas kyis// khams gsum gnas dang lam lngar 'khor// de nyid log rtogs sna tshogs snang // de las ma gtogs gang yang med// ye nas ma bcos zhes bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ blo med byang chub smon mi dgos// 'gro lnga ma lus thams cad kun// ye nas byang chub snying por gnas// de bzhin dbyings kyis kun du khyab// ji lta ba yi ngang gnas la// de ltar rtogs pa'i blo 'jug pas// gnyis su med par rtogs 'gyur na// su zhig bcos shing su yis rtogs// rang bzhin 'od gsal zhes bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ chos rnams ma lus thams cad kun// rang rig ye nas dag pa yi// sus kyang ma bcos ngang gis gsal// ma chags pad+ma 'dra ba yi// ye shes can gyi spyod yul de// kun dang thun mong de ma yin// de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod yul de// skyes bu blo rtsal rab kyis rtogs// thams cad dbyings phyug ma zhes bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ mi zad yon tan gter gyur pa// zad pa'i dus med yid bzhin mdzod// bdag dang bdag gi med pa yi// shin tu zab pa'i blo las byung // chos dbyings zab mo'i don rtogs na// sku dang ye shes bsam mi khyab// rang rig ye shes don rtogs na// skye shi med pa'i g.yung drung thob// byang chub sdom byed ces bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ gzung 'dzin bral ba'i ye shes kyis// chags med dbyings la mnyam bzhag na// thams cad de bzhin nyid kyi zhing // nyon mongs sdug bsngal 'byung mi 'gyur// chos kyi rang bzhin ji lta bur// bdag gis yang dag rdzogs byas te// theg pa dman dang phyin ci log // thams cad mnyam pa'i dbyings su dgod// phyogs dus gnyis med ces bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ phyogs bcu dus bzhi thams cad kyang // rtogs pa'i mtshan ma so sor snang // snang ba nyid na dbyer med de// mtha' dang dbus med zlum po yi// de bzhin rang gis rig pa yang // mtha' dang dbus med du ma min// gang du mi 'gro kun du khyab// kun la bde sbyin mi gnas pa'o// thams cad 'byor ldan zhes bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ chos rnams so sor rtogs byas shing // thams cad gnyis med dbyings shes na// mi zad par ldan rgyan thob ste// kun du zad med rin chen gter// de bzhin nyid la gnas bcas na// nyon mongs sdug bsngal mi 'byung ste// rtag tu bde gnas byang chub nyid// mtshan dang dpe byad kun dang ldan// thabs gnyis shes rab ces bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ ji ltar snang ba thams cad kun// thams cad thabs kyi rang bzhin te// thabs la thabs ni rnam par sbyor// sbyor dang sbyor ba gnyis ka med// sna tshogs snang ba thams cad kyang // snang ba nyid na rang bzhin med// de nyid shes rab yin par bshad// rtag tu thabs nyid mi dmigs pa'o// shes rab nyid la thabs su sbyor ba zhes bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ de bzhin nyid kyi dbyings nyid las// rol ba sna tshogs cir yang 'byung // 'byung ba nyid na rang bzhin med// med pa nyid na sna tshogs snang // thabs dang shes rab dbyings las byung // mnyan bsams bsgoms pa'i shes rab kyis// shes rab thabs su don rtogs byos// kun la de ltar 'byor par gyis// gnyis med byang chub sems zhes bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ thabs dang shes rab ldan 'gyur na// gnyis med byang chub sems 'phros na// kun gyi 'byung gnas byed pa po// de yis ma byas gang yang min// kha dog dbyibs rigs gang yang min// shin tu brtag dka' sus mi rig // bdag gis bdag kyang mi mthong na// gzhan gyis rtogs par ga la 'gyur// thams cad sbyor byed ces bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ ye nas lha dang lha mo yin// dkyil 'khor yang dag sbyor ba dang // dbang po yul du sbyor ba'o// phung po lnga nyid de bzhin gshegs// 'byung ba lnga nyid yum du sbyor// dus bzhi'i lha mo nyid du sbyor// rtag chad mu bzhi khro mo'o// thams cad ma lus 'byung ba kun// mnyam pa'i dbyings dang rig par sbyor// yang na shes rab dbyings ma la// bder gshegs dkyil 'khor kun bkod la// bdag nyid rig pa'i lhar bsgoms te// gnyis su med par ldan par bya// rdo rje dril bu ldan gyur nas// byang chub pad+ma shin tu spro// phyogs dus dkyil 'khor mnyes pa dang // 'gro ba mang po bde thob nas// slar yang gnyis med dbyings su bstim// thim 'gyur dbyings nas phyag rgyar 'bar// bder gshegs thabs dang shes rab rdzogs// phyag rgya drug kyang yang dag rdzogs// bsod nams tshogs chen gnyis kyang rdzogs// thams cad dbyings su 'byor pas na// ngan 'gro mi ltung yang dag 'grub// 'di ni bsgral ba chen po yin// sgrol ba nyid ni sbyor ba yin// sbyor ba nyid ni ma lus bsgral// thams cad ma lus par sgrol byed ces bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ phyi nang snod bcud ji snyed pa// gnas pa'i sems can ma lus kun// bdag nyid chen por rtogs pa yis// dbyings su yang ni bsgral bar bya// shin tu khro bo chen po yis// thabs kyis lha chen bsgral ba ltar// chos nyid rtogs pa'i ting 'dzin gyis// gnyis su med par thabs kyis bsgral// thugs rje chen po'i byin brlabs kyis// lam lnga'i sems can kun bkug nas// thams cad ma lus bsgral bar bya// ri rab chen po'i gling bzhi la// gnas pa'i sems can ma lus kun// thugs rje chen pos byin brlabs te// ye shes me chen bsgom byas na// thams cad ma lus bsreg par bya// dbyings su yang ni bstim byas te// de bzhin gshegs par byin gyis brlabs// rgyal ba'i sras su dbang yang bskur// de ltar bsgral ba kun byas kyang // bsgral ba'i dngos po gang yang med// phung po lnga po bshig pa la// bshig nas 'byung ba bag la zha// ma bshig na yang 'byung ba yin// rnam shes med pas bsad byas na// gnas pa nyid na dngos po med// sems kyi rang bzhin de la ni// dus gsum sangs rgyas dgrar langs kyang // sus kyang mi zin sod pa med// 'o na thugs rjes gang bsgral na// rnam rtog mtshan ma thams cad kun// phyin ci log las bzlog byas te// ting 'dzin sngags dang phyag rgya dang // shin tu goms pas dbang bskur te// byang chub zhing la dgod par bya// de tsam la ni bsgral zhes gdags// bsgral ba nyid na sbyor ba yin// nyon mongs sdug bsngal rtsad bcad nas// byang chub gnas su bsgral bas na// gnyis med dbyings su sbyor ba yin// thabs nyid shes rab shes rab nyid thabs te// gnyis su med pa nyid byang chub kyi sems so// sbyor ba ni lha dang lha mor sbyor ba'i dkyil 'khor dang / dbang po yul dus sbyor ba dang / chen po lnga de bzhin gshegs pa lngar sbyor ba dang / so so rtsal sgyu ma tsam du yod pa yum du sbyor ba dang / dbang po yul dus lha dang lha mor sbyor ba dang / rtag chad mu bzhi khro bo khro mor sbyor ba dang / mngon sum du sbyor ba'o// sgrol ba ni thabs kyis sgrol ba dang / 'pho bas bsgral ba dang / dus bzhi mnyam pa nyid du bsgral ba dang / thams cad ma lus par dbyings su dus gcig bsgral ba dang / thams cad thugs rje chen pos gnyis su med par sgrol ba'o// 'di gnyis dus gcig tu mdzad de/ ya char ma gyur par bya'o// dngos grub mchog kyang der thob ces/ de bzhin gshegs pa nyid la de bzhin gshegs pa nyid kyis bshad do// ma byin par len pa zhes bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ 'jig rten 'das dang 'jig rten pa'i// chos rnams ma lus thams cad kun// bdag dang bdag gi gzhan na med// rang bzhin rang gis bdag med pa// kun la thogs med spyad 'gyur yang // spyad dang spyod pa gnyi ga med// thams cad ye nas stong pa la// gang gis len cing gang la spyod// snang srid ma lus thams cad la// thogs pa med pa'i spyod 'gyur yang // bcing par mi 'gyur bsod nams tshogs// chags med ye shes chen po yin// ma lus thams cad chos kyi dbyings// de ltar rang rig yin par bshad// gnyis su med par rtogs gyur na// blangs pa nyid na kun du bzang // du smra ba zhes bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ chos rnams ma lus thams cad kun// ye nas dngos po yod ma yin// rang bzhin ngang gis 'od gsal la// ming tsam tshig gis mtshon mod kyis// ming dang tshig la dngos po med// ma rig pa yi 'khrul rtog gis// nga dang bdag tu med pa la// so so mtshan ma dngos por bzung // 'dzin pa'i dngos po yong med de// chos rnams thams cad ming tshig tsam// ji snyed mang po brjod pa yang // rjod par byed dang brjod pa med// chos rnams thams cad du snang // nyid la ni spyod de// zhes bya ba btags pa tsam// thams cad gyi tshig yin no// rdo rje 'joms byed ces bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ thog ma med nas phyin ci log // bdag dang bdag gi med pa la// rnam rtog mtshan ma so sor 'dzin// 'dzin pa'i dngos po yod ma yin// mi mthun mtshan ma gzhom pa'i phyir// rdo rje lta bu'i ting 'dzin gyis// bdag rtog bag chags kun bcom nas// rdo rje dbyings su thim par bya// chos kyi 'khor lo zhes bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ thugs rje chen po'i byin brlabs kyis// khams gsum nyon mongs 'khor ba rnams// gzhan gyis bcings te 'khor ba min// 'dzin rtog chags pa nyid kyis 'khor// blo chen rab tu ldan pa yis// chos kyi don po mchog nyon la// 'khor ba spang med sangs rgyas zhing // thams cad ma lus chos nyid rtogs// rin chen 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ nor gyi mchog ni dkor bdun yin// 'dod pas btsal bar mi rnyed de// sku gsung thugs 'das mi dmigs pa'i// chags pa med pa'i tshul gyis ni// gnyis su med par 'byor byas na// nor bdun chen po 'byung bar 'gyur// mtshan dang dpe byad sna tshogs ldan// pad+ma chags med ces bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ 'jig rten 'das dang 'jig rten pa'i// chos rnams ma lus byang chub zhing // don rnams bsgrub pa zhes bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ rdo rje rigs kyis thams cad bcom// rin chen rigs kyis yon tan 'byin// pad+ma rigs kyis chags med 'gyur// sku gsung thugs dang ye tshul bzhin du// sna tshogs kha dog dbyibs su snang // de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung rnams ni// sgra dang ming tshig kun las 'das// brjod med rang bzhin kun du go// nyon mongs med cing bla med sgra// ma lhun grub sangs rgyas chos// sgyu ma'i tshul du kun la spyod// spyod med ngang gi dkyil 'khor la// chags med tshul du rnam par rol// bya byed rnam pa sna tshogs kyang // byed pa nyid na chu zla'i bcud ma lus thams cad la// snang ba chen pos khyab par 'gyur// nam mkha' gzung du med pa ltar// snang srid thams cad de dang 'dra// chos rnams thams cad sems yin te// sems ni nam mkha'i rang bzhin no// rten byed sa chen zhes bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ ji ltar sa gzhi chen po la// sems kyis zin dang ma zin pa'i// skye 'khrungs ma lus thams cad 'byung // thams cad kun gyi gnas brten te// de bzhin theg chen bla med la// byang chub sangs rgyas kun kyang gnas// theg pa mtho dman thams cad 'byung // thams cad theg chen dbyings su 'dus// sreg byed ye shes me zhes bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ bdag med ye 'khor bar 'gyur// mnyan bsams bsgoms pa'i shes rab kyis// bdag med gnyis ni rtogs byas na// pha rol phyin rdzogs sa bcu bsgrubs// sa gsum yang dag rdzogs byas te// mnyam pa'i zhing la thams cad 'god// khrus kyi mchog ni 'di yin no// g.yeng byed chen po zhes bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ sems can ye nas dag pa la// bdag 'dzin rdul snyed g.yogs par 'gyur// sems dang rdul rnams med rtogs pas// ye shes rlung gis bag chags gtor// chos rnams ye nas rlung dang 'dra// de la gzung du med pa ltar// kun la de ltar 'byor par gyis// ma bcos ye nas de ltar gnas// thams cad kun la dbang sgyur zhes bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ rang rig phyin ci ma log pa'i// gzung 'dzin gnyis med rtogs pa yis// thams cad mnyam pa'i ngang 'gyur na// thams cad ma lus bdag yin pas// thams cad kun la dbang sgyur te// ji ltar dmigs pa bzhin du 'grub// ji ltar spyad kyang bsod nams tshogs// mnyam rig ye shes chen po yin// chos thams cad gzugs brnyan ltar shes par bya ba'i dam tshig ni// thams cad 'byung ba'i gnas yin te// snang ba nyid na 'ja' tshon bzhin// rang bzhin med par kun du snang // de nyid chos sku yin par bshad// cis kyang ma gos ma spangs pa'o// so sor snang zhing mthun pa'i gzugs// bdag dang bdag tu ma brtags pa// de lta bu yi ngang du snang // chos rnams sgra ltar shes par bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ sgra rnams ji snyed brjod pa yang // dngos po med las dngos po sgra// brjod dang sgra yi dngos po min// chos rnams sgra ltar shes par byos// thams cad ma lus don 'byung ba// tshig gis mtshon pas gud na med// sgra nyid don gyi dngos po min// don nyid sgra las gud na med// chos rnams dri'i mtshan nyid du shes par bya ba'i dam tshig ni/ chos rnams thams cad dngos med par// sna tshogs 'byung zhing rnam par 'phro// de bzhin dri yi dngos po yang // yod pa ma yin kun du mnam// the tshom med pa'i shes rab kyis// chos
